In Hermes, it has a Kanban feature.

I like Notion because it eliminates the disk usage that AI models can create.
But if you don't want to use Notion, you can use Kanban or you can use Obsidian.
But you make a very strict rule with your agents that they have to, before they start, they have to document what they're going to do and they basically have to open that ticket.
The ticket can be a Kanban ticket, like normal, or it can be a new Obsidian page or a new Notion task.
It's very specific. They have to create this and the person who creates it is the team lead.
That's how I have mine set up.
They have to create sub-agents who work on specific pieces of the task.
Each agent has to close out their ticket.
They cannot close it out unless it is documented and marked closed.
If there is a blocker, there is a strict rule.
You have to create a sub-agent to fix the blocker and get rid of it.
Or you have to tell the human exactly what is wrong and how the human needs to fix it to unblock.
Do not continue, do not leave it open, do not make something up.
I make sure it knows, those are strict rules.
This basically creates a very good system that holds your agents accountable.
They'll create those tickets.
If it runs into a block, it comes to you and it tells you, hey, we can't move forward.
I need you to do this.
It won't lie to you and tell you like, oh, no, we fixed it and it's good to go.
You will see exactly what you have to do to unblock your agents.
It pauses your sub-agents, waits for you to respond.
And then once you respond that the blocker is moved, it continues with those agents.
It unpauses them, lets them continue on their task.
And then it finishes the task, documents, it closes, and it moves on.

We have epics, we have sprints, and we have accountability.

Don't naturally bond their velocity creates thermal pressure
A constant outward push that resists any attempt to organize them into a stable structure
Elite engineering talent operates under the same mechanics
Specialized genius and demand for autonomy create a high pressure state that naturally repels corporate oversight
They stay in independent orbits burning through energy without ever forming a cohesive unit
Most startups attempt to solve this with standard recruitment ping pong tables and standard vesting schedules
But these external perks have no mass
They fail because they cannot exert a force strong enough to overcome a maverick's deep desire for independence
in astrophysics
The gene's mass defines the exact threshold where a gas cloud becomes so dense that its internal gravity overpowers its thermal pressure
Once this limit is crossed the cloud collapses inward eventually igniting into a star
Attracting elite mavericks requires a similar structural approach
You must build a gravitational anchor an objective with enough systemic density to pull independent actors
Out of solo orbits into a shared high-velocity core
The density of that anchor depends on the difficulty of the problem
For this project the constraint is the architectural failure of local first artificial intelligence
Modern hardware can run powerful cognitive models on a tablet or a local desktop
But the moment a user switches devices or tries to synchronize vector memory with a peer
The local first promise breaks down to manage state developers rely on a centralized cloud a corporate data harvest point
That's just a cloud app with a delayed fuse. We must build a zero knowledge sync protocol
Pure peer-to-peer rails make data completely invisible to any routing server
This cryptographic constraint acts as the perfect honeypot
It is a brutal systems level puzzle that standard corporate entities are not incentivized to solve
It provides the initial mass for the gravitational anchor
To maintain this pole the organizational structure must balance three forms of gravitational mass
The first pillar is ideological mass
This requires framing the work as an unsolved epic rather than a corporate goal
The manhattan project utilized this principle in 1942
Before the project began figures like enrico fermi and richard feinman were independent gas clouds
Scattered across various academic orbits
J robert oppenheimer recognized that capturing these mavericks required an objective so dense it could crush personal academic rivalries
The mission was a profound existential paradox with a ticking clock
Discover the fundamental mechanics of the universe before an authoritarian regime could weaponize them
Today solving decentralized zinc carries similar weight
Framing it as a historical necessity to prevent a corporate monopoly on ai data provides the mission level density needed to anchor elite developers
The second pillar is paradoxical mass elite operators are often trapped by the administrative friction of their own success
Consulting contracts billing systems or the limits of a solo agency the anchor offers a structural trade-off
By entering the event horizon of the collective they surrender absolute personal freedom in
